"American Grit" aired from 2016 to 2017 as a reality TV series that showcased civilian contestants undergoing military-style training. The program's military trainers, collectively known as "The Cadre," consisted of Navy SEAL instructor Rorke Denver, U.S. Army veteran Noah Galloway, Marine Gunnery Sergeant Tawanda "Tee" Hanible, and Army Ranger sniper Nick "The Reaper" Irving. Through a competitive format, the series tested contestants' physical and mental fortitude, highlighting the attributes that embody "American Grit."

<br>

## 70. [Teen Choice Awards](https://serp.ly/amazon/Teen+Choice+Awards)

![Teen Choice Awards](https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/3q900BNcKbe3GHga4RVxSnoiqP4.jpg)

<br>

The Teen Choice Awards is a Fox-presented ceremony honoring annual achievements in music, film, sports, television, and fashion, as voted on by teens aged 13-19. Since its debut in 1999, this summertime celebration has featured numerous celebrity appearances and musical performances, awarding winners with authentic mini surfboards. The event has since inspired several YouTube spin-offs, making it a comprehensive showcase of teen culture and its impact on various entertainment fields.

## 71. [Manhunt](https://serp.ly/amazon/Manhunt)

<br>

When reality television took a thrilling turn in the summer of 2001, UPN's "Manhunt" brought viewers an adrenaline-fueled competition like no other. Contestants raced against time as fugitives on the run, with actors portraying relentless bounty hunters in pursuit. The stakes were high for these eight episodes filmed in the picturesque Griffith Park - though the show claimed to be set in Hawaii. It's a captivating look at how far people will go for glory and a cash prize in this memorable but brief series.

## 72. [EP Daily](https://serp.ly/amazon/EP+Daily)

![EP Daily](https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/4wQ09bVS37rxD3UqzUJZ8beaNsh.jpg)

The first and best TV series about the videogame industry, now served daily with more cool info about the entertainment and tech that gamers love.

<br>

"EP Daily" is the pioneering TV series covering all aspects of gaming culture, from movies and TV shows to comic books and collectibles. Hosted by Victor Lucas through his production company Greedy Productions, this daily news program has been a gaming enthusiast's companion since 1997, offering insightful looks into the industry's impact on entertainment and technology.
